    8698             : /**
    8699             :  * For space efficiency, we collect finer resolution for small difference
    8700             :  * between net and cache time, coarser for larger.
    8701             :  * Bucket #40 for a tie.
    8702             :  * #41 to #50 indicates cache wins by 1ms to 100ms, split equally.
    8703             :  * #51 to #59 indicates cache wins by 101ms to 1000ms.
    8704             :  * #60 to #68 indicates cache wins by 1s to 10s.
    8705             :  * #69 to #73 indicates cache wins by 11s to 60s.
    8706             :  * #74 indicates cache wins by more than 1 minute.
    8707             :  *
    8708             :  * #39 to #30 indicates network wins by 1ms to 100ms, split equally.
    8709             :  * #29 to #21 indicates network wins by 101ms to 1000ms.
    8710             :  * #20 to #12 indicates network wins by 1s to 10s.
    8711             :  * #11 to #7 indicates network wins by 11s to 60s.
    8712             :  * #6 indicates network wins by more than 1 minute.
    8713             :  *
    8714             :  * Other bucket numbers are reserved.
    8715             :  */

    8717           1 : nsHttpChannel::ComputeTelemetryBucketNumber(int64_t difftime_ms)

    8720             :                 std::lower_bound(positiveBucketLevels,

    8725             :         return difftime_ms >= 0 ? 40 + absBucketIndex
    8726           1 :                                 : 40 - absBucketIndex;
    8727             : }
